Maximillian von Blitz

An entourage of various peoples surround the man as he sits back down on his throne. A few minutes later he dismisses them with a nonchalant flick of the wrist. A notification appears in the sights of every contestant, glowing similarly to their personal document. For a few seconds it shines, “We are free to speak.” The stairs leading up to the throne are largely emptied of people and none but the blond man sitting atop the central throne can be found on the highest level.

arrow_drop_down# Thonk, Thonk, Thonk

Hovantis

Thonk, Thonk, Thonk

The stranger’s boots echoed on each step made of the staircase. An impending metronome of the stranger’s arrival.

Thonk, Thonk, Thonk

A hefty clunk is made as they relieve their shoulders of their pack’s weight, dropping it to the floor. Standing before them now was the man known as Hovantis. They smiled kindly upon you and the majesty of space. “The Sea of Stars. Their infinite beauty is somewhat diminished having been made the object of another’s conquest.” A depressive air washes over them.

“I’ve walked a long way to come here. It appears I’ve arrived under-dressed.”

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

"The beauty of any flower is not lessened by its gardener. There is always a keeper. In man's absence, such responsibilities fall upon the stoic orders. We have merely given nature a moment's reprieve in Our conquest. Someday it will reclaim its throne after I am gone." Maximillian smiles. Raising his free hand, he gestures to the man's body. "You have arrived nonetheless. Attire can be arranged. Or not, if preferred. That which defines your world's champion is not Our place to say."

Hovantis

Hovantis’ mustache curls with his widening smile. “The champions you do not define, but the given roles & rules, you certainly do. Or do you mean to imply we are truly free to act as seen fit. I wonder.”

Upon being offered a wardrobe change he accepts “If you’ve made the offer It would be rude to refuse. It’s been a while since I was able to dress up for celebrations after all. My current attire carries too much of an air of solitude over my weary shoulders to truly let loose. I’ll trust your tastes in the chosen attire for the festivities at hand.”

“Ah,” Hovantis catches himself as he came here with purpose “but it would seem I’ve already ascertained the inevitable answer from you I was seeking. Nevertheless, it is still one question worth musing. I would ask you to define what is perfection.”

Maximillian von Blitz

A light tap of the butt of Maximillian's scepter against the ground beside his feet rings out rhythmically, echoing to the music emanating from the blond ruler. A faint ring made of a fuzzy golden light descends down from a thin column of radiant light, eventually stopping at chest level with Hovantis. "A gift from Us to you. An artifact belonging to another ancient wayward traveler. On one's right hand, an outfit of your own inspiration. On one's left, an outfit of another's hope or image for you. So long as eye contact is shared when putting on the ring." A light chuckle escapes him. "It has on occasion brought Us entertainment. Even if it is not always active."

Should Hovantis put the ring on his left hand while staring at Maximillian a spectacle of golden lights will shimmer all across his body, transforming his attire into that of an appropriately classy black suit.

"As for your inquiry," the man sits upright on his throne, pulling his head back in a slight sideways tilt as if he was asked a question he had never once pondered before, "perfection is the greatest sum of all flaws. An order of disorder, a beauty refined until broken, a dirtiness cleansed by its collective missteps. The multiverse was beautiful before Our arrival and it will be beautiful upon Our departure, but Our finality will mark a return to order of which time will not allow repair."

Hovantis

“I see. A very human response delivered in an equally inhuman way. I would have expected no less from the keys of this world.” The stranger spoke not out of malice but in acceptance of the given answer. “Not an answer I’d wager is acceptable to the other champions. But I am not one of the other champions. And they are not me.” The stranger spoke matter of factly, leaving little room for interpretation. A window of time was allowed for a rebel retort, but it hardly seemed necessary for one of western sensibilities.

Hovantis slides the gifted ring over his left, and in a dazzling flash!... whisking away the mustached fellow’s tacky hat and cumbersome pack to the shadow realm, his fashion sense rejuvenates! Into a dashing luxury suit with complementary stunning shades! No lesser quality than befitting von Blitz themselves of course. The humble traveler removes the shades, and then his top notch blazer. Pocketing the former and slinging the latter over their shoulder. A slight change in their demeanor could be noted now. The mysterious stranger’s kind smile turned to a content one. A kurt, no thrills, sayonara was uttered to you, and then the man went on his way.

Clack, Clack, Clack

A lengthy halt brings the pattering of their departure to a still silence…

“This game. Our perfection.They are irrelevant to a wandering traveler. The mission of my journey has not changed. I shall do as I please in my time here.” Hovantis turns around after breaking his stride and looks back up the fleet of stairs to von Blitz.

“It is only luck that our journeys cross paths.”

“It is only honorable that I thank you for this brief reprieve.”

“Arigatou.”

The man tilted his head in a bow so slight it was not appropriate for even the meager status of a middling banker, but the tone in the man’s voice. That last second, gravelly desecration. Echoing harshly throughout their every fiber of being. It rang ragged, hollow, and weary, befitting only of fifty five thousand lifetimes of sleepless nights.

Clack, Clack, Clack

The mysterious stranger departs

Maximillian von Blitz

During the pause, Maximillian offers an agreement rather than a retort. "As you say, they are not."

Nothing is said as Hovantis turns to make his initial leave. Rather, the ruler's expression alone says all that is needed to be said. A smile of contentedness, a gaze relaxed by unfaltering confidence, and a posture both commanding and somehow unimposing in this brief moment. Satisfied.

At the wanderer's halt, as if their whispers could be heard across the entire hall, Maximillian softly says, entirely audible despite their distance and the commotion in the hall, "Fortune's benefactors boast mercy. Destiny's, themselves." After his thanks the lights in the main party hall dim and the next song begins to play.

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# A destined encounter.

Destiny Dude

Destiny Dude approaches the golden haired man sitting on the throne, when he opens his mouth to speak he does so on an loud and annoyed tone "You must know what happened, even if you look like a person, there's no way are from the same species...How can you be so vile as to even joke about putting one of the few, if not the last remnant of human civilization on the Milky Way galaxy? And just for a game!?".

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

Offering a light smile, Maximillian replies calmly, "Your presence before Us is no trifling matter. It is one of nearly an infinite number of steps to attain Our perfect universe."

Destiny Dude

The man looks even more irritated. "Do you really not care at all? what do you mean by perfect universe!? you are just destroying billions and billions of lives, and you think promising somebody a prize would make up for all of those you've killed? no matter if you promise them all the gold and diamonds on all the star systems, it would still not be enough!"

Maximillian von Blitz

Continuing to match the Dude's anger with tranquility, Maximillian continues calmly, "On the contraire, Our care for the multiverse is immense. How could We be uncaring of that which We've seized through the greatest conquest in history? There would be no sin less forgivable than settling as idle overseers, unwilling to mold existence with the authority ordained to us by fate itself into something greater."

Destiny Dude

"And you do that by playing games? it sounds like an excuse to torture powerless people. Even the reward for 'winning' this game sounds like a bad joke, what does it mean to be granted one request? what if this Architect cannot grant it?"

Maximillian von Blitz

"We have established this trial which pulls from the subconscious of entire worlds. Agree or not, your own have nominated you their champion. They are none the wiser of whichever fate befalls them while simultaneously responsible in their entirety for your presence before Us. If the agency gifted to you is a burden then curse those you wish to protect." His eyes narrow, smile fading just a smidge. "We are Maximillian von Blitz, Architect of Perfection, Ruler of All. You may address Us as you so please... The impossibilities of the victor's request are intrinsically tied to the impossibilities of the multiverse. If We cannot make it so then such a request is impossible by all accords."

Destiny Dude

He mumbles more to himself rather than to speak to Maximillian."I was chosen...is this why I survived?...there is a chance to fix everything?" He shakes his head. "You really tell the most sick jokes." At this moment Destiny Dude seems to be more worried about whatever conversation with himself is happening inside his head rather than waiting for Maximilian to keep the conversation going.

Maximillian von Blitz

"...You are preoccupied." Maximillian dismisses the Dude with a refined wave of the hand. "Go. Affirm your resolve, chosen champion of Earth. If you desire dialogue with Us once again We are not difficult to find."

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# The char walks up to the throne

JaneetChairson

The chair walks up to the throne and pauses for a moment completely awe struck. "U-um, A-ah, excuse me, sorry I am just not used to seeing moving humans on non moving chairs. Its completely backwards! But excuse me sir, have you seen my daughter by chance? I'm afraid of what will happen to her if I've gone missing."

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

A refined gaze falls upon Janeet. His eyes study her as if she were any ordinary human. A relaxed voice of nonchalant confidence replies, "Only you were chosen by your world to be here before Us. In consolation, We are confident your fates are intertwined."

JaneetChairson

"I-intertwined? Well wouldn't she be here with me if we we're intertwind? Or would I be fated to see her again? I fear of what Chairster will do to her if I've gone missing"

Maximillian von Blitz

A light smile forms on Maximillian's face. "A fear held by many, yet one of no import, awaits those who fail. That is, nothing. In success your daughter will be before Us. A fate with no greater security. Seize victory if your anxieties need assuaging."

JaneetChairson

She frowns in deep thoughh for a moment. before locking eyes with Maximillian. "So you are saying. The key to escaping that evil Chaister. I just have to win so my daughter can come here?.......... Away from Chairster, the pain, and maybe to be of more worth than just my body. Is to win? To win this game?"

A grin shoots across her face. "That seems like a challange I can do, I will get my daughter back and finally escape Chaister!"

Maximillian von Blitz

His smile widens ever so slightly before dissipating altogether. With a refined flick of the hand, the ruler dismisses Janeet. "Now that We have invoked motivation you must act upon it. Go." His voice is imposing, yet somehow encouraging all the same.

JaneetChairson

The back of her chair moves forward as if to nod, motivation filling her face. "Will do!" She then turns to the crowd and walks towards them.

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Concerning Gods and Men

Shul'N'Zuroth

Slowly starting up the stairs, a middle aged man with unkempt hair and his bright purple robe looks upwards at the man on the throne. Giving a large yawn, his empty hands stretch, seemingly a normal human until from out of his robe emerges a tentacle holding a cup of coffee and handing it off to his hand. Z takes a sip, finally reaching the throne and giving a sigh."

"So just to make sure, this isn't some challenge of the great old ones where I'm stuck in a dream within a dream within a dream? It's happened before"

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

Maximillian's mouth curves into a sudden smile, almost as if stifling a mere chuckle. "We assure you that Our presence is no illusion. Contrary, your inclusion signifies an undeniable importance that any deity of your world would be envious of. The agency bestowed upon you encapsulates a reality more tangible than any you have ever known."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Z lifts the coffee cup to his lips drinking deeply before giving another sigh, this one seemingly of relief.

" Well I suppose that's good at least. Still just...who or what are you to have such powers and sway with the universe to be able to assemble all these people and construct such a vast creation such as this. Are you saying that you are an even greater holder of power than the Elder Gods whos reach and influence spans the cosmos?"

Maximillian von Blitz

The man relaxes back into his throne. "We are Maximillian von Blitz, Architect of Perfection, Ruler of All. Our power is unmatched. Every universe, including yours, was conquered long ago. The Elder Gods you speak of are either inferior lurking powers at be, survivors of the Great War, or fabrications of an entity belonging to one of the two prior."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Z's grip on his coffee mug tightens and his brow furrows at the words of the man on the throne. He opens his mouth as if to speak before stopping, seeming to think at length about his words before taking a final sip of coffee, handing his empty cup to his tentacle which retreats back into his robe.

*"What is to happen of the winner of this 'game' then? Do they return back to their home and just continue their existence?"

Maximillian von Blitz

"Those who are victorious will be granted eternal passage aboard Prosit 13 and may bring with them up to 30 others from their world." A beam of light shines down, forming a column of radiant glory between Maximillian and Z. In it, a hologram-like depiction forms, showing a three dimensional animation of a tournament bracket of featuring various Earths. "Your triumph will carry your world into the next round, and so on until it is the final Earth or until it is destroyed. Returning to your world, should it ultimately prove the most perfect, is something We allow. Though, the odds are astronomical."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Gritting his teeth Z begins to step towards the throne, angrily stomping up the stairs. You can see a variety of tentacles writhing out of his robe now as he lifts a finger towards the man on the throne

*"You would truly destroy and alter the worlds of billions? Take the lives of uncountable innocents? What of our families? My wife, my children, the family members of those who didn't even have a chance at this opportunity? And for what exactly the pursuit of perfection? I was happy in my world, loving life excited to greet each day with a smile and a yawn and you would take that from me? From all of us?"

Maximillian von Blitz

"Yes." Maximillian's response is short and delivered as a matter of fact.

Shul'N'Zuroth

"I've spoken to Shoggoth more empathetic than you. You're a monster and some day you will get what you deserve"

With a quick turn of the heal Z storms off tentacles trailing behind him forming the shape of a hand flipping the bird at Maximillian

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Annoyed Bird Lady

Seseri

Practically the moment that the stairway is cleared, Seseri swoops down from above and lands a few feet away from Blitz, crossing her arms and stomping up to him in an obviously angry manner.

Once she reaches him, she starts tapping her foot impatiently, before turning to gesture to the rest of the grand hall. Moments later, she lets out a loud call, a small pulse of light shooting off from her in all directions as she does.

"Fweet!?"

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

He stares for a few seconds before smiling and closing his eyes. "I suppose We have made inadequate accommodations." He lifts his free hand and loudly snaps his fingers. A beam of radiant light begins to shine down between him and Seseri. Slowly descending through the column of light, befitting the magnificence of the holy grail itself, is a simple pen and paper. As soon as it is grabbed by Seseri the pillar of light vanishes.

Seseri

"Fweet? Fweet!?" Seseri lets out several more angry trills, stomping her foot dramatically as she does so, before snatching the pen and paper out of the air. She starts furiously writing down on the page, nearly ripping it in the process, before shoving it into Blitz' face.

"Who the hell are you and what did you do with my exploration partners!?!?!!? You should be lucky I know how to write in the Ancestor's language!"

Maximillian von Blitz

His eyes open and his smile grows, amused. "We are Maximillian von Blitz, Architect of Perfection, Ruler of All. You may address Us as you so please... The denizens of your world have subconsciously proclaimed you their champion. Such is not Our place to question. Should you seize victory your comrades and yours existence will be ensured."

Seseri

She turns to the pen and paper for a moment before looking up to the air above them. Moments later, she looks to almost deflate, letting out a high-pitched sigh. A few moments later, she turns back to Blitz, a new message in hand.

"Why though? What's the point of all this? If you're as powerful as you make yourself sound, what could you possibly hope to gain from all this?"

Maximillian von Blitz

"We had seized the universe," a beam of radiant light shines down once more between them, this time containing a moving hologram-like depiction of a scene showing an epic space battle and flashes of various ceremonies and celebrations, "and yet hungered still. The greater multiverse became Our next obsession. Such conquest occupied Us for a time, but, too, was eventually seized." The imagery before Seseri changes, now depicting world after world being obliterated by numerous means, magnificent and not. "In Our boredom we sought perfection. A universe of only the most perfect worlds. Champions hailing from throughout the multiverse contend to prove their world's worth. In time, only one of each world shall exist and Our perfect universe finally be seized." The sights shift, showing various Earths. "The world, Earth, is now under examination. Most Earths have been destroyed, but many more are yet to be vanquished. Your victory will guarantee your Earth's continuation in this examination. Perhaps its eventual place in Our perfect universe will be owed to your efforts." The beam of light disappears along with its various depictions of Earth.

Seseri

Seseri listens to the man's explanation silently and without any outward reaction. Once he finished, she silently took to her notepad once more, calmly closing the distance between the two and handing him one more note, her glow, far brighter than it had been before.

Once she handed him the letter she silently took off into the sky.

"Perfection is impossible. And you, Maximilian von Blitz, are a monster."

Maximillian von Blitz

Maximillian's amused expression does not wane. He watches as Seseri flies off and then returns his gaze to the stairs before him, awaiting any more who should approach him.

Hail to the King

==================== <:Blank:879835071740256276> <:Blank:879835071740256276> NIGHT 1 TRANSPIRES <:Blank:879835071740256276> <:Blank:879835071740256276>

arrow_drop_down# An Unusual Query

Ami Muscaria

Ami slowly approaches the throne, seeming to take in every detail of her surroundings. Her wooden sandals make light scuffling sounds with each dainty step. A few feet from the blond-haired man on the throne, she lifts one white-gloved hand toward her face and lets out a faint cough before addressing him,

"You must be the captain of this... ship, I suppose? I apologize if this seems rude, but there's a question I have to get off my chest. You wouldn't happen to be the crew who dropped a strange box on the earth about 30 years ago, would you?"

Maximillian von Blitz

Music emanates from the sitting man. https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0IrirVIEhMQ

A relaxed smile paints the man's face. "We are Maximillian von Blitz, Architect of Perfection, Ruler of All. You may address Us as you so please... Your mysterious box is unknown to Us. I am doubtful my fleet is responsible."

Ami Muscaria

"Hmm..." Ami nods slightly and cocks her head to one side. "Very well, then. If I may ask, what is the end goal of your quest for perfection?"

Maximillian von Blitz

"After having seized the multiverse, Our greatest desire was the perfect universe. One filled only with only the most perfect worlds. If We are destined to possess an infinite beauty, why would We not cultivate it into its most remarkable form?" Maximillian sits upright, assuming a more strict pose. "Destiny has ordained Us the arbiter of existence. It is Our right, Our responsibility to shape what is into what should be."

Ami Muscaria

Ami shakes her head and sighs. "Ahh, everything gets more confusing by the second." Lifting a hand and offering a slight wave, she quips "Thank you for your time!", before she turns around and begins to descend the stairs.

Hail to the King

==================== <:Blank:879835071740256276> <:Blank:879835071740256276> NIGHT 1 TRANSPIRES <:Blank:879835071740256276> <:Blank:879835071740256276>

Archibald Don Castro

The well dressed gentleman begins to occasionally spasm, particularly around his upper body. “Mmmm? Not too fond of crowds are you, Cedric?” He peeks inside his arm sleeve. “Ha! I suppose I can’t blame you. This is quite the colorful menagerie we have here.” Archibald disperses from the crowd and takes a seat by himself at a table.

arrow_drop_down# Curious Ami Approaches

Ami Muscaria

"Mind if I have a seat at your table, sir?" Ami asks politely, tilting her head in the count's direction. "You have quite the interesting sense of style, if I may say so. What do you think of our current... situation?"

Archibald Don Castro

“Be my guest.” Gestures Archibald to a nearby seat. Initially he doesn’t look directly at Ami, but once he does, he’s immediately taken aback. This doesn’t last thankfully and he resumes his composure. “Golly. I’ve really seen everything, haven’t I? First a bird lady, now a mushroom lady…” He mutters to himself.

“I appreciate your compliment! My take the utmost care of my attire. Looking my Sunday best is what gives me vigor.” He booms enthusiastically. “As for our predicament, I hold a similar sentiment to most of our fellow shipmates. This is inexcusable. To be thrust away from our homes for this rubbish is a crime against humanity!” The Count comments with disdain. “That said, I do intend to return to my world. My daughter will not be taken away from me! Likewise you have loved ones you wish to ve reunited with, don’t you?”

Ami Muscaria

"Yes, there are several people I hope to see again very soon," Ami replies. "Where I'm from, people either have plant growths, animal appendages, or some other strange mutations. It's a culture shock to see so many... normal looking people around."

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Curious Yumi Approaches

Yumi Dae

Yumi emerges from the crowd shortly afterward. "Aha-ha! Looks like you, my fine stashed friend, were able to sneak a friend upon this here ship! Tell me, if I may ask a question or two and a moment of your time?"

Before Archibald has ample time to respond, however, she lands herself plumply onto a chair at the table. "I've always wanted a pet, the idea had been romanticized in the books of the past, yet it has always been taboo because of the food shortages."

"Where you hail from, does everyone have someone like your Cedric?"

Archibald Don Castro

The man politely welcomes the unfamiliar woman. “Salutations, miss. I’m happy to indulge your questions. Provided they're the reasonable sort, of course.” He chuckles. Cedric peeks out briefly to inspect Yumi, but disappears just as quickly.

“Yes, this is Cedric, my shy animal companion. I suppose ferrets are not exactly common pets compared to cats and dogs, but the concept of owning animals is not foreign where I come from. It’s quite a shame you’re not afforded the same luxury. The idea of animals being restricted purely as a resource sounds quite tragic.” Suddenly the gentleman clasps a hand over his forehead. “Oh where are my manners? Seems I didn’t properly introduce myself yet. I am the third Count of the Don Castro family, but please just call me Archibald. Even Archie is fine. I’m not opposed to nicknames.” Archibald bows his head slightly. “May I have the pleasure of knowing your namesake, miss?”

Yumi Dae

When Cedric makes a brief appearance, Yumi's face lights up as her eyes track Cedric. Her eyes beam with joy, and her mouth agape with excitement.

She straightens her posture trying to return to a more professional look "Oh-! Yes, of course. It'd be nothing but daft of me to skip the introductions, wouldn't it?" She extends her hand for a handshake. "Yumi Dae, Director of the South Section 3 of the Chi Association. A pleasure to make your acquaintance, Archie." A subtle change in her tone suggests she's said this countless times.

She resumes her previous mannerisms. "Well, mostly I was curious about this Cederic and how you were able to get him aboard this ship. But now you've piqued my interest again; It seems like you come from an influential family in society. Might I ask what role you filled just a few days ago?"

Archibald Don Castro

The Count accepts the handshake without hesitation. His grasp is noticeably gentle. “Pleased to meet you as well, Miss Yumi.” Archibald appears impressed upon the mention of her position. “Ah, so you’re a director! Sounds like the busy kind too. I’d say this break of routine might’ve served as your holiday, but the dire stakes as said by that head honcho there speaks otherwise.” To avoid branching over to a potentially uncomfortable subject, he clears his throat and changes topic back at Yumi’s inquiries.

“Cedric here appears to have been simultaneously escorted with me when that Max fellow whisked me away. Why it was him and not, say, my butler Wayne… I cannot tell. Probably for the better as Cedric fares poorly without my company.” Archibald ponders the new question posed by Yumi. “My role. Well, I was piloting my airship, the Aubergine, to deliver a speech to New Gloucester. This aircraft is nothing to sneeze at, but it pales to the magnificence of my Aubergine! Anyways, basically I’ve been touring the world to influence, assist, and inspire hope among the less privileged of society. Someone has to look out for the smaller people in life, I say.”

Yumi Dae

Yumi nods in approval with your answer. "Ah, an airship! I've yet to see one with my own two eyes~ Must have been *quite *extravagant to best this one."

"Y'know, I'd always thought that the world could always use more people like you... Using their power and influence to better the world, not shape it to their whims. You've got a noble cause and the power to act on it. I've always strived to be like that myself, but it's a difficult journey to the top. You're a good man, Archie. Friend or foe, I am glad to have met you like this."

Archibald Don Castro

“Well I’d never admit my pride and joy is inferior to this ship, technological advancements or otherwise. That’d be sacrilege!” Archibald scoffs with a smile.

The Count’s smile continues upon being praised by the young woman, though it dims over time. “You flatter me, Miss Yumi. Honestly… I just wish I woken up much sooner. If only I recognized how vile and selfish my original ‘friends’ who take advantage of so many people. Who not only excommunicated me but refused to help my wife Gwendolyn, whose health was in decline, and then she…” Archie stops midway, rubbing his eyes periodically. Eventually he continues. “My apologies, Miss Yumi. We stumbled upon a sensitive area. Needless to say, I was once part of aristocracy, full of naïveté and ignorance. So I can’t help but partially blame myself for aiding the problem. Even as I intend to undo the curruption I was blind to, this is something I’ll never forgive myself. Sigh.” He looks at Yumi gratefully. “Sorry for blathering like that. I appreciate you lending an ear. I too am glad to be acquainted with you. Despite any potential revelations, I intend to remain on good terms with you.”

“Now, what kind of world are you part of? I’m quite curious considering its harsh attitudes towards owning pets.”

Yumi Dae

Waving her hands back and forth "No no, no worries at all Sir Archie. Lending an ear is the least of my worries."

Inquisitively she begins, "Now now, would you like to hear about the beginning of the end, or start at the current state of affairs?"

Yumi thinks to herself for a moment. hmmm "Both are generally heavy topics, but i find neither personally sensitive. If you're in the mood for such an account, I'd be happy to elaborate. No pressure though"

Archibald Don Castro

“Hmmmm. I suppose the beginning of the end? Hearing about the origins always piques my interests. Well, Miss Yumi, I’ll be your audience!” He turns his chair to face the young woman directly.

Yumi Dae

Excited to recount the tales of her people, Yumi continues "Yes! Of course. I hope you don't mind some dramatics 😉"

"Today, I shall treat you with the tale of my people!"

"The Ten days of Twilight, as it is now known began with a dawn that never came." Yumi extends her pointer, pointing towards the heavens. "Before the sky had risen, the sky began to shimmer a subtle translucent blue. Soon after, bright rays of sunshine filled the sky, but alas the sun had not moved. This, my friend, was the beginning of the end."

DRAMATIC PAUSE

"The people of the three cities that remain today had known no better at the time. But those who found themselves outside what seemed to be a barrier, were all too aware of changes that had occurred. First electronics stopped working. I'm sure you know what that means; critical infrastructure failures, loss of communications, and of course the great loss of information and the internet."

"By the second day, there had been 24 hours of twilight in the cities. People realized and panic set in, but nobody could come or go. By the end of the tenth day of twilight the sun finally rose upon the cities. But alas, it was too late. In just 240 hours, half the earth came became scorched, the other half frozen. Completely uninhabitable."

"The magnetic field of the earth lost composure and cosmic rays began to beat down upon it. The results of this phenomenon are what my people call the corruption. I of course, explore the corruption and exterminate monsters within! The rest, however? History!"

Archibald Don Castro

While the Count follows Yumi’s story, he gives subtle reactions of intrigue, shock, concern, and puzzlement. The last emotion stuck once the girl finishes.

“You seem… unusually cheerful describing what sounds to be a near apocalyptic hellscape. That said,” Archies expression softens, “I think it’s good to have someone as enthusiastic as you are. Imagine how dour things would be if everyone held the same hopeless, cynical demeanor. I’m sure you act as the heart of your team being the director. Now, what kind of monsters do you normally encounter?”

Yumi Dae

"Why yes! I think I'd be quite problematic to kill the mood with a sob story of my world. People love tragedy, and this is no different..."

Yumi pauses briefly, almost as if reconsidering what she's about to share. "Besides! I was born way after the event I'd just described so its all pretty normal to me.

Yumi takes a moment to explain the following flow chart and how she approaches her problems:

"The monsters? The come in all shapes and sizes. Many are humanoid, some are gargantuan, and others tiny. Anything you can imagine, there's a good chance its out there. No two creatures have been quite the same though. The worst ones are those that work together. I've lost good men from smart monsters. Nothing to do but learn, adapt, and never get complacent."

"Theres a saying, what was it?-- tsc tsc tsc tsc-- Ah! Quick on your feet, hard to defeat."

teet teet teet!

Juliana Kitchener

arrow_drop_down# Curious KFC Approaches

Seseri

Seseri practically skips up to Archibald, fweeting excitedly at him. "Fweet? Fweet Fweet!" she looks up at his arm sleeve, angling around to try and have a look inside.

Archibald Don Castro

“Now now… be careful mis-… hmmm, whoever you might be?” The Count appears apprehensive about the Seseri coming so close. “I don’t want you frightening Cedric and cause him to bite… oh?”

yip yip!

Excited sounds come from within Archibald’s coat. The ferret pops even its head out and doesn't appear intimidated by the bird person. yip!

“Well I never! Seems like my Cedric has taken a liking to you!” Marvels Archibald, “That’s quite rare. Perhaps you two are able to communicate?” The gentleman examines Seseri with a puzzled expression. “Interesting. A avian humanoid. Is it even possible to talk with this being?”

Seseri

Seseri giggles softly as the Ferret comes out to greet her, fweeting at him excitedly. It's oddly melodic, almost as if someone had superimposed a wind chime on top of her laughter.

After Archibald mentions talking with her, however, she suddenly straightens up, letting out a higher-pitched noise. "F-fweet!" Reaching down to her paper, she excitedly starts writing stuff down.

"Thankfully, I can understand your language! I still can't believe I'm seeing living Ancestors in the flesh... I'm Seseri. What's your name, Ancestor?"

Archibald Don Castro

Relieved upon learning that communication with Seseri was not a lost cause, the gentleman wastes no time introducing himself. “The pleasure is mine, Miss Seseri. I am Count Archibald Don Castro III, but simply Archibald will suffice. An ‘ancestor’ you say? I only have a daughter. Not sure I’ve started a lineage long enough to be referred as that.” The Count chuckles dryly. “Are human beings rare or even extinct where you come from? Also, if you’re able to tell me, I’m curious to know what kind of conversation you had with Cedric. If you could understand him, of course.”

Seseri

Seseri lets out a low, mournful trill as she writes, before handing Archibald a note.

"Extinct, I'm afraid... when the darkness fell your people were among the first to go, according to surviving records. No one is sure why. By the time the planet sent forth the Daysprings to give us light and warmth, your people were long gone. Your people are called the Ancestors because you came before, and we call ourselves Descendants because, among other things, we came after you."

"As for Cedric... he's drawn to the light inside of me. Our Light springs from the planet itself, natural and warm. It was gifted to us by the Springs when the Darkness first fell so we could lead the remaining life on our planet to safety. And yeah, I can understand him! We mostly just introduced ourselves, he says hi to you by the way."

Archibald Don Castro

Archibald solemnly reads along. “I see… so my kind was a doomed species in your world. What a pity. In some sense, I wonder if it was brought upon themselves. Humans are capable of doing some of best things and the worst things. I know this since I’m afraid I’ve heard and encountered some very bad people in my life. I wonder if this was judgement by…”

Not wanting to sour the mood, he changes the topic back to his pet. “Well I’m glad you’ve made a friend of Cedric. I’m envious of your animal communication skills in fact! It’s quite the gift. He might not look it, but he can be a real rascal sometimes! Just the other other day I left my bubble tea out while I doing an errand and this scamp-” Tetetetetetete! You could hear what sounds to be animal like laughter coming from the mischievous ferret. “Yes you! You drank every last drop! What am I to do with you?”

Seseri

Seseri laughs loudly as the two banter, sending out the odd pulse towards Cedric which earns clearly amused yips in return. "Fweet! Fw-Fweet!"

Once her laughter has calmed down to giggles, she straightens out her wing feathers before putting pen to paper. "I won't say that's an uncommon theory amongst our people. The shroud that covers the world outside of spring-side cities is known to be thickest in Ancestor Cities, having explored them myself you can practically taste the cold and decay in the air. Some have taken that as proof the Ancestors somehow brought it upon themselves, others say that it's proof that an outside entity focused on the most dangerous targets first. *And those are only the two most popular theories, all we know is that your people were probably involved in some way, good or bad. For better or for worse, your people were long dead by the time we were uplifted from doves."

"Cedric says it tasted delicious, by the way!"*

Archibald Don Castro

“Oh did he? I would never have guessed! Not even my daughter would be so cheeky.” The gentleman pouts indignantly as Cedric continues chattering.

Engrossed by the lore shared by the avian lady, Archibald appears resigned upon hearing the possible outcomes of his people’s extinction. “I see. So there are multiple theories. Alas, I don’t foresee this mystery being solved anytime soon. Still… it must be exciting to meet me. I’m not the only human here, as you might’ve noticed.”

Seseri

"He reminds me of the chicks back home! From the sounds of it, your own chicks can also be pretty mischievous huh? Reminds me of what Yaki, Tori and I got up to in the academy."

Looking around at the various humans in the room, Seseri lets out an excited chirp. "It definitely is! I've spent my entire life studying your civilization but I never thought I would get to meet any of you in the flesh! Well... alive, that is." Seseri grimaces. "My 20th hatchday is in a month, and my partners Yaki and Tori both turned 20 earlier this year. We've been venturing out into the shroud for a few years at this point, though only as official explorers for about one and a half. Still, none of us are used to the sight of your empty, frozen streets. I don't think we ever will, It's incredibly eerie."

Archibald Don Castro

“Yes, my daughter is quite the handful. Bright and lovely girl, but still cheeky. As I put her into a private school in British India for a resplendent education as well as safety, it’s been several months since I lost saw her. Hopefully she hasn’t held a grudge about that. Despite my many letters to her, replies have been on the sparse side. I suppose she’s in that rebellious age. If you’re curious about her looks, there’s a picture of her that I keep in my pocket.” He reaches inside his coat and pulls out a small framed photo of a young girl. “This is Cynthia, my lovely child. She means the absolute world to me.”

Upon her mention of exploration the Count appears quite impressed. “You’re one for adventure too, eh? And someone so young as well. It’s big world out there. No better use than to make it your oyster and learn something of it! It’s wise that you brought along trusted companions as well. I always had my butler and good friend Wayne to be my right hand man. I’m sure he’s handling my Aubergine quite well in my absence.”

Seseri

"It's been my dream since I was a chick! my nestmates have never approved due to the danger, but pah. What do they know?"

Seseri tilts her head, letting out a curious trill, with a certain cheeky ferret chitting back. "Tell me more about your daughter and Wayne?"

Archibald Don Castro

“Gladly! Wayne is my personal butler and close friend. We met while I was studying in Oxford. He’s originally from the United British Principalities of American, but transferred to Great Britain as a student. He’s not a refined butler like most. He’s boisterous and rowdy, and fully speaks his mind. A man I need in my life to make sure I don’t lose track of myself.” Archibald nods with a grin.

“As for my daughter, she’s my only child. Cynthia is sweet girl, and one to like sweets herself. That’s where her mischief comes in! If I ever found a box of cookies or a gallon of ice cream completely empty, she will no doubt be the culprit. She also enjoys fashion, socializing, and video games like most children her age. Sadly, her attitude has become gradually choleric. Not to the point of being a spoiled brat, mind you, but it’s obvious my Cynthia has… changed. Perhaps my daughter is just ‘that age’ as she’s in mid teens now, but part of me wonders if her mother’s passing… that is to say my late wife, had something to influence her behavior. I fear sending her to school in India might not have helped her mood either, but I genuinely that was the best coarse of action for both her education as well as her potential safety. I sure hope you haven’t had to deal with the untimely loss of a family member. You never really feel the same afterwards.”

Seseri

"I lost my pa to an expedition gone wrong at an early age... the grief never really leaves you, does it? Seems that's something in common between us, at least." Seseri lets out a low, mournful trill.

"You would send her away? wouldn't isolating her from all she knows just further dampen her mood?"

Seseri tilts her head, resting her chin on her knuckle. "Butlers... if I recall, they're like assistants, right? I'd certainly hope a person like that would speak their mind. What would the point be otherwise?"

Archibald Don Castro

“You lost your father at an early too? My condolences.” Archibald shakes his head sadly. “You can never truly take the kives of others for granted. Mine passed when I was roughly in my teens. He was a stern man, much more than I, but he was never abusive or cruel. The death was due to old age. When I was conceived my father was well into his mid 50s.”

The Count sports a guilty look when Seseri brings up her insight concerning Cynthia. “Truth be told, I always wondered if that would be the case. Even with the letters I frequently send her, her replies are uncommon in return. However,” He resumes his composure “That’s not to say I regret my decision. Cynthia has friends at her school, is apparently doing a great job academically, and most importantly in an environment that is safe. I’m unhappy that I might’ve furthered deepened a rift, but I have hope she’ll forgive me in time. I live a more hazardous life than you realize, and the idea of losing another loved one is unbearable. Surely that’s understandable?”

Archibald snaps his fingers. “Exactly! Wayne is more or less a personal helper of mine. Compared to me who prefers to play it safe, he’s more of a risktaker. When he staunchly believes in a certain action, I almost always take it. Sure enough, they usually pay off. Having a ‘yes man’ would result in stagnation and false assurance. I know too many such people when I was once part of the Midas Club.”

Seseri

*"The two of you compliment each other and in doing so you achieve more than either of you could do alone. It's common back home, out of sheer necessity in the face of outside threats.

As for my own pa, as I said, he was lost to an expedition gone wrong. We don't know the full details - as is, unfortunately, very common - but none of his fellows returned... We all know the risks. I myself nearly died on my first mission, it was only through the quick thinking of my partners that I returned home alive. Let's just say Ma wasn't too happy - she's been awfully protective of me and my nestmates since Pa died."*

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Barely a hello

Henry Hoover

Henry watches Seseri run warily. He holds a cigar in his mouth and pulls out a gold-plated zippo lighter, trying, and failing, to feed his addiction. He momentarily catches Seseri’s eye and he smiles thinly, holding up a hand as a greeting, before continuing to fiddle with the uncooperative lighter.

Seseri

A quick flap of her wings later, and Seseri has landed in front of Henry, fweeting at him enthusiastically. Taking a moment to regard the cigar, she quickly brings out her pad, jottling down on it for a second before handing it to Henry.

"Can I hold that... thing for a second? what is it?"

Henry Hoover

Henry is barely able to disguise his grimace. He looks at the bipedal bird and back to his obviously expensive cigar.

"Sure... Just be careful, I want it back" He finally says.

"It's something I use for recreational purposes, and I imagine they're gonna be hard to coime by here"

Seseri

She picks up the cigar, holding it gently in her hands and regarding it idly. Given it already looked big in Henry's hands, the cigar looks absolutely massive in Seseri's. After regarding it visually for a moment, she lifts her mask slightly from the bottom, putting the Cigar close to her still-covered face. After a moment she physically recoils back, hastily handing the cigar back to Henry.

Henry Hoover

Henry shrugs. "Probably for the best, they're not for everyone. These things will probably kill me long before anyone here does." Henry laughs at his own joke.

Seseri

"What's in that thing? Poison? it smells like it..."

Henry Hoover

"You're half right. Everyone at home sure seems to think so." Henry waves his hand in a dismissing motion. "Listen. Forget about the cigars, we're getting off topic. What's your deal?"

arrow_drop_down# A Welcomed Sight

Ami Muscaria

For a brief moment, Ami makes eye contact with Seseri and, beneath her mushroom cap, her eyes widen in excitement as she moves closer to the bird. "Hey there! You seem excited to be here. Can you still speak a human language?"

Seseri

"Fweet? Fweet Fweet. Fweet?" Seseri seems hesitant to approach Ami, but hands her a note nonetheless. "To be here? No. I left my partners stranded in the middle of the shroud because I was plucked away to be here and I have no way back. As for languages, we talk in other ways. Pulsing, mostly. We were never human to begin with."

Ami Muscaria

"Ah, I'm sorry! I did not mean to offend you," Ami says, bowing slightly. "For some reason, I assumed you were a human-bird hybrid, as I see them often back home. Who are these partners you were with? I imagine it must've been a bit traumatic being pulled away from them like that."

Seseri

Seseri tilts her head heavily sideways at the mention of 'human-bird hybrids', letting out a soft, low fweet once Ami finishes speaking.

She takes out her pad and starts scribbling with it. A minute later, she lets out a frustrated sound and practically rips the paper out, crumpling it up and stuffing it into a pocket. She proceeds to do this several more times before visibly deflating, and the next paper is given to Ami instead of being crumpled.

"Human-bird... hybrids? Assuming you mean the Ancestors, no. Your people have been extinct for centuries where I'm from. As for my partners... they're Yaki and Tori, my partners in crime! We've been together since our first year in the academy, playing pranks, training together and basically anything else you can think of. The three of us were asleep when I was plucked from my spot between their wings by jerkface on his throne over there."

Ami Muscaria

Ami lets out a slight gasp and puts one hand up to her mushroom cap, approximately where her mouth would be. "I wonder what caused humans to go extinct in your world... given what has happened to mine, it's surprising people are even still around."

"You mentioned the academy - were you in the military before, or more of a scholarly type?"

Seseri

"More of the latter, I guess, but closer to a bit of both. We trained to become explorers, hardened survivalists who can venture out into the shroud and survive. The scholarly aspect comes in studying what is out there, mostly the remains of Ancestor structures... but that's where the shroud tends to be thickest, so it's extremely dangerous. Most human cities are swarming with the corrupted and visibility is so bad even our own internal lights barely do anything. That same shroud is what killed off your people - without the internal light we possessed you had no resistance against the darkness. It killed you from inside out."

She lets out a soft, mournful trill.

Ami Muscaria

"Oh my... that's terrifying," Amy replies somberly. "What exactly is the shroud? Is it a creature or a landscape?"

Seseri

"We're... not sure of the full specifics. We know it's covered most of our world, that it kills and warps anything without light to resist it and casts an endless night upon the land, with only the areas near the spring having any light at all. But we don't know if it's alive or if anything's controlling it."

Ami Muscaria

"That sounds very similar to the Altering on my world... they say it started out as a sort of pixelated fog that eventually seeped into everything and spread out across the globe. It happened before I was born, so I didn't witness any of it, but it's something beyond human comprehension."

"Do you get taught a lot about your Ancestors back home?"

Hail to the King

Grug

The caveman begins sprinting about the room at incredibly high speeds. He zooms over to many a strange artifact held in a case, sometimes stomping his feet repeatedly when he arrives at a particularly interesting one, before another catches his eye and he runs off towards it. He glances towards the other strange contestants before whipping his head back to the other curiosities. He doesn't seem to have any immediate interest in talking to anyone as he falls to the ground and rolls on it, running his hands over the spaceship's floor before rising to his feet and doing the same to its walls. By this point he is panting, an excited look in his eyes as he looks around.

arrow_drop_down# A Dog's life....

Destiny Dude

Destiny Dude studies Grug's movements all over the room, at first he was on guard from the caveman's erratic behavior but once he realized doesn't look too violent Dude shakes his head and says. "...Maybe you've been blessed."

Grug

Grug seems to be able to hear what the man of destiny said, and heads over to him, but stays a few feet off. "Grug has been blessed! Grug and all others here, chosen to visit the abode of the Gods!" He seems a little excited, and wears a smile.

Destiny Dude

Dude seems a little surprised Grug can speak. "Gods? I would call them demons, they are planning on destroying all of our home worlds for the sake of their games."

Grug

"They will not destroy Grug's home! Grug is mighty! Grug will protect his home and win!" He pauses. "You have... Grug's condolences about your home though." He casts his eyes down.

Destiny Dude

Destiny Dude's face softens as bit. "Heh, thank you. Even if we have opposing interests, I wish you luck."

"I wonder if I should take a page out of your book, at this point there's no reason to fight this fate after all, doesn't it?"

Grug

"Grug and you are chosen by the Gods, fighting back is an impossibility, so we must fight for our homes!" He pauses. "Why is your skin dark? Have you spent too much time in the sun?"

Destiny Dude

Blinking a couple times he says. "I may have, and that's why I am having this weird fever dream with all of you in it. Does everybody in your home look the same as you?"

Grug

"No, there are some who are taller. Some are mightier. Some are shorter, some are thinner, some are weaker. Some are women, and Grug is definitely not a woman. Some men have longer beards, but Grug endeavors to keep his short to avoid it being scorched by flames. Some who spend more time in the sun come back with skin which is darker, not near as much as yours... though some who spend too much come back home red." Grug chuckles.

Destiny Dude

"Nobody as dark as me huh? did you get to know many other people or just those who live near you? Also, it doesn't seem you were one of the ones who spend much time under the sun."

Grug

"There are no other people near Grug's tribe." He says flatly. "Grug and his tribe and all the world were cursed for our ancestors actions, who pulled at godhood, so the gods struck them down, and their anger continues to this day. Or perhaps it did until they brought Grug here..."

"Grug used to leave home more often, but was given the high honor of staying back at the cave and tending to the fire. For 93 moons Grug has been the one to tend the fire."

Destiny Dude

"So you are a cave dweller, maybe a bit more of sun and grass can do you some good instead of just staring at a fire all day."

"From where I am from people that look like me are not rare at all, there are probably others as dark as me living far away from where you live, maybe if you come back alive to your tribe you may one day meet them."

Grug

"Don't Grug know it!" He says in response to the first remark.

"Truly? Amazing! So people with your skin just are? You are born with skin such as that instead of like normal?" At this point Grug has approached and seems to be disregarding personal space as he reaches out to grab a hold of one of the man's arms, trying to get a better look.

Destiny Dude

He reluctantly lets Grug study his arm. "Yes, besides being a darker color than yours, my skin is not that different."

Grug

"Iiiiincredible!" He releases the man and steps back. He then glances down at the rusty piece of metal in the man's hand. "That looks like one of the ancestors' creations, old, brown, flaky, hard."

arrow_drop_down# Squakin to Grug

Seseri

Seseri practically squawks as Grug runs by, hastily jumping out of the way before staring out in the direction he ran off in. She continues to keep an eye on him as he continues to run, getting out of the way of any possible collisions beforehand.

When he finally stops, she takes off into the air, gently landing next to him moments later, note in hand. After fweeting at him in an annoyed fashion she hands him the note.

"Hey, you nearly knocked me over! be more careful n~~o~~ext time!"

Grug

Grug looks at the note. "Grug is amazed! Astounded! Scratchings upon this item entail meaning, meaning which Grug can somehow comprehend!" He jumps straight up and down, barely bending his knees, springing off the balls of his feet. He rotates the note back and forth in the air, looking at it up and down, before glancing down at the small bird person.

"Small bird person!" Without any warning his hands jolt forward to Seseri and he runs his hands through her feathers, sometimes sort of grabbing but not pulling.

Seseri

"F-fweet!" Seseri makes a shocked noise as the larger man suddenly reaches out for her, practically jumping out of his grip. Once at a safe distance, she stares up at him for several moments before putting her hand to her chest and taking a deep breath, idly reaching over to adjust her mask as she does, before reaching over to her wings and slowly starting to put the misplaced feathers back the way they were.

Grug

"Oh, no," Grug looks downtrodden, and frowns, before squatting down. "No, return to Grug, smart little bird person," and he whistles, a 'fooweet' sort of noise.

Seseri

Looking up at the man, Seseri heaves a sigh before approaching the man once more, written note in hand.

"Please be more careful with my feathers! I can feel from those, after all. Playing with them too roughly hurts."

Grug

Grug looks over the note. "Oh, Grug sorry. Grug had no intention to harm you, smart little bird person." He drops the note on the ground sort of carelessly. He stands in front of the bird girl sort of awkwardly before once again extending his hands more slowly to try and feel her feathers.

Seseri

Seseri simply lets him play with her feathers, letting out a barely audible as she starts to write down on her pad once more. "You know, where I'm from it's considered rude to play with another's feathers like this without permission." Seseri chuckles softly. "It doesn't stop young chicks, though. Where are you from, Ancestor?"

Grug

Grug pauses when he hears it's rude, then pulls a little on his own chest hair. "Hm. Perhaps it would be rude to do such to me... ancestor? Grug is not your ancestor... Grug thinks?"

Seseri

Seseri chuckles softly once Grug finishes speaking. "It's... complicated. We call your people Ancestors because you came before us. We are the Descendants because we came after."

Grug

"But... how did Grug and his people come before you when Grug and you are both here now?"

Seseri

"We're from different Earths entirely. Who's to say we're all from the same time periods? I wouldn't worry about it too much, Grug." Seseri giggles softly.

Grug

"Grug supposes that is true." He nods. "Were you ever like Grug, or have you always been a bird?"

Seseri

Seseri shakes her head softly, scribbling down a note and handing it to Grug. "Our people are said to have descended from Doves, so we've always been like this."

Grug

"Doves? Those little 'coo'-ing birds? Amazing! Those taste goo-" Grug catches himself. "Grug's apologies."

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Attempt at Communication

Ami Muscaria

Suddenly, Ami catches Grug's wild movements out of the corner of her eye, and she finds herself completely spellbound.

He can't be... a caveman?? she thinks to herself, leaning closer to get a better view.

She cups her hands around where her mouth should be beneath her cap and shouts "HELLO! SIR?!"

Grug

The caveman glances over at the mushroom headed person as she shouts her greetings. He cautiously approaches, but stays about a meter or two away from her, and he sniffs the air. He seems to not want to get close. "So this is why Grug was informed by his elders to not consume the red-capped mushrooms..."

Ami Muscaria

Ami giggles and shakes her head. "Yes, the primary mushroom that grows from me is what you'd call 'red-capped', but when they are not attached to a person, they don't speak or anything. They make you very sick if you eat them, though."

She awkwardly scratches the back of her head and speaks a little quieter, "I only called out to you because you seemed to be looking for something."

Grug

"Hmmm... Grug is unwilling to take his chances, for he wishes not to... have a mushroom grow from himself."

"Looking for something?" The caveman asked. "No, Grug is looking at something! Look, so much to gaze upon! Things Grug has never seen! Strange things! Amazing things!"

Ami Muscaria

Ami takes a look down the hallway, and outside one of the vast windows, taking in the vast beauty of the space surrounding her and lets out a pleased sigh.

"Admittedly, it is rather beautiful and awe-inspiring here. Have you gone to speak to the man on the throne yet? He's in charge of this whole thing."

Grug

"Grug has many queries! But there is so much more for him to see! Grug would not bother the man until he has seen even more and has more questions to put upon that man all at once!"

Ami Muscaria

"Good luck trying to get the answers you seek out of him," Ami says. "How do you feel about being here - aside from being surprised by all the strange things around you? I bet this is very different from home!"

Grug

"Amazed! Grug is pleased to enjoy the company of those chosen by the Gods!" He looks out the window. "Behold, it is like the night sky, but more! All over! And inside, there is so much!" Once again he goes to the ground, running his hand over the floor. "Grug has never felt something like this before!"

Ami Muscaria

It all makes sense now, Ami thinks as she nods along to what Grug is saying.

"What was your home like? Where I'm from, everywhere is surrounded by many plants and strange animals, and many people have... gifts, I suppose. Gifts from heaven, you might say!"

Grug

"Grug and his tribe spend much time hiding from the eyes of the Gods, not wanting to be seen and punished for our ancestors' transgressions."

Ami Muscaria

"Interesting," Ami leans closer and looks up at Grug curiously. "What transgressions did your ancestors commit to drive their descendants into hiding?"

Grug

"We are told that they tried to reach the Gods, and so they were struck down. To this very day, the Gods smite the land from their heavens... though now that the Gods have chosen Grug, this will surely change!"

Ami Muscaria

"Well, for your sake, I hope your theories are right," Amy sighs. "I'm afraid things are not going to be that simple."

Grug

"Why not? Grug is not merely mighty, but also a genius!" He flexes with one arm while with the other he points to his head with one finger.

Ami Muscaria

Ami tilts her head back in laughter. "Haha! I don't doubt your intelligence, Mister Grug. Did you get into a lot of battles back home, then?"

Grug

"Battles? No, there is no one for Grug to fight against. Grug has not been on a buffalo hunt in a while either."

Ami Muscaria

"Are there any other people where you're from, Grug?" Ami asks, a hint of concern in her voice. "It sounds like you've had a lonely life."

Grug

"There are plenty of others in the tribe, but Grug has never met any outside of it. Grug's life not lonesome at all."

Ami Muscaria

"Oh, well I'm very glad," Ami says heartily. "Have you met any of your Gods before?"

Grug

"No? Gods would smite Grug for the ancestor's transgressions! Was that unclear?"

Ami Muscaria

"Ahh, I see. That makes sense to me now," Ami replies, smiling warmly.

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# A Tentacled Handshake

Shul'N'Zuroth

"I'm glad to see I'm not the only one appalled at our current situation"

Shul'N'Zuroth approaches the embittered man slowly, a cup off coffee clasped in both hands, he raises it to his lips, taking a sip before standing next to Destiny Dude.

"Pleased to make your acquantaince. I'm Shul'N'Zuroth but you can call me Z" He says a tentacle snaking outward as if offering a hand shake"

Destiny Dude

Destiny Dude looks at the tentacle but he doesn't shake it."Who wouldn't be? they are treating to destroy whole planets just for their enjoyment..." He takes a short a short pause before continuing. "I'm not sure if I'm losing my mind or not, but knowing that not everybody is on board with this ridiculousness makes me feel like I am not a complete lost cause yet." his frowns turns into a melancholic faint smile for a second.

"My name is not important, feel free to call me any way you want."

"I'm sorry but I am not sure how I should act while talking to things that..." He glances at the tentacles peeking out from Z's form. "...that are not human, I didn't even know there were other intelligent creatures besides just my species."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Z chuckles a bit, handing his coffee cup to one of his tentacles before grabbing his robe and lifting it up, revealing a mostly normal pair of legs and feet. Tentacles do continue to writhe and slither idly as you them originating from what must be his back

"I am human if you'd believe it. Simply blessed by the Elder gods. Azathoth to be more precise as this is his gift. My family has spent their years devoted to his worship and...well his dreams. Do the Elder god's reach your world too?"

Destiny Dude

He frowns his eyebrows a bit. "Elder gods? I've only heard of stuff like this in fantasy and sci-fi stories...." with a sigh he goes on. "So this is a dream after all? ...I figured it was going to happen sooner or later, but to think that crazed hallucinations could feel so real."

Realizing he has been more talking to himself rather than answering Z's question he clears his throat. " Uh, no. No Elder world has reached any world I know. But at this point I guess most of them have already been destroyed by humans..." he shakes his head. "No need for any power beyond my comprehension for that to happen, just plain old greed."

He looks at the tentacles again. "If you don't mind, how did..." He points at the tentacle. "That happen?...you know, the Elder god thing."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Z's eyes light up a bit at the question gulping the last of his coffee down before handing the empty mug to his tentacles.

"Well, my friend, as I mentioned it was a gift from the great ones, specifically Azathoth. In ancient times at the dawn of we were chosen by the old ones for a grand task"

Z holds out his hands and a tentacle snakes from out of his robe to hand him a large aged scroll. Alien rune-like markings cover it and as he speaks you can see a faint light glow over them

"Humanity would worship the Elder gods, and in return we would receive their gifts and blessings. Some families, like mine, decided to receive the greatest of gifts, a mixing of bloodlines and so Azathoth, the great dreamer's blood runs through my veins. These are a mark of his favor and love"

Z takes a moment before taking a breath and stuffing the scroll back away in his robes

"Please forgive me for that heh. I get a bit excited talking about the old one's and their history. It's been my life's work documenting it and deciphering their teachings and iconography."

Destiny Dude

He shakes his head. "There's no need to apologize, I was the one who asked in the first place."

"If your people got chosen for a grand task then how are these elder gods going to react to...whatever this is? from the looks of it your world may also be in danger."

Shul'N'Zuroth

Z yawns before nodding, agreeing with the sentiment as his tentacle snakes out from his robe pouring hot water from an electric kettle before another adds instant coffee and cream stirring it all together

"I haven't the slightest clue how the Elder ones are reacting to all this...this all feels like a...I'd say dream but I'm all to familiar with dreams. This is a nightmare"

Z sighs letting himself indulge in the warm cup of coffee before speaking again

"I shudder to think how this will affect all our worlds, the innocent lives that are affected...and I dare not think about how I may never see my loved ones again...whatever the case this sick game is vile and disgusting. And I'll have no part of it if I can help it. Care for some coffee by the way? I've got tea as well."

Z offers as several other tentacles produce an additional mug and a box filled with packets of assorted teas and instant coffee

Destiny Dude

Destiny Dude takes a deep breath. "If this is a dream, I suppose there is no point on being angry the whole time; it's been a long time since the last time I tasted some good coffee, thank you for the offer." He reaches for the mug accepting the invitation. "I hope I'm not prying to much in asking how your world is, you mentioned loved ones and you seem like a well mannered person, so I assume it is a nice place to live in."

Shul'N'Zuroth

"Not at all! We're thriving in fact" The tentacles reach out offering sugar and cream while filling the mug with hot coffee

"The Elder gods certainly don't look a thing like us, nor do their offspring but they've given humanity a variety wonderful gifts. Technology that we've taken and improved upon over the years. That's why we have things like this. Just need to make sure they stay juiced up"

Z says knocking on the side of the electric kettle before reaching into his robe before producing a small vial. You can see now on closer examination it's made of a strange bone-like material with grooves and edges carved into it. A swirl in the center of this glows red, which Z starts to fill as he opens the vial letting the thick viscous liquid poor into the cracks. The symbols and grooves start to fill and glow as if sucking up the liquid til all the grooves are full again.

Z puts the vial back into his robe as the tentacles slink back into his robe hidden away again

"Just gotta keep a little bit of blood on you to keep the small stuff running"

arrow_drop_down# Cheerio from a Count

Archibald Don Castro

Taking noticed of the disgruntled man’s countenance, Archibald walks over to Henry. “I don’t blame your bad mood. This predicament this Maximilian chap thrust upon us is unsettling to say the least.” Something seems to occur within the Count and his eyes narrow. “You look… familiar. As if I saw you on a cover of a magazine or tabloid. Perhaps I’m losing my marbles but…”

He notices the golf clubs. “Aha! You must be a professional golfer. How many series have you won?”

Henry Hoover

Henry’s eyes snap up, pulled away from his thoughts. His hard-set frown melts into a warm smile as he laughs, tickled by some inside joke. “None yet, friend. And I’m no professional, I only got into golf over a pissing contest with my favourite person to annoy.”

Henry’s eyes quickly scan Archibald up and down, as if taking inventory of something.

“And I have been in more magazines than I can count, so who knows?” Henry’s signature frown returns once more, tugging slightly at the corners of his lips. “Although, I get the feeling that you and I are from very different places”

He extends a hand: “Name’s Henry. Henry Hoover. A pleasure”

Archibald Don Castro

“Cheers! Count Archibald Don Castro. The feeling is mutual.” He gently shakes the hand of Henry. The mention of Henry having a rival amuses the gentleman. “Now I get it! It’s your way of sticking it to the man. That I can respect. There are many people I wish to bring down a peg or two. Everyone in that bloody Midas Club. Frivolous corrupt simpletons. ahem” He catches himself going on a potential tangent and clears his throat.

The Count nods. “I concur. We are unlikely to come from the same place. That said, perhaps where we come from only has minor differences compared to the other guests here.” Appearing intrigued, Archibald rests his hand in his chin. “So, if golfing is merely a hobby yet you’re notorious enough to be on magazines, what might your true profession?”

Henry Hoover

Henry coughs awkwardly and breaks eye-contact for the first time.

“I sell vacuum cleaners.” He says, growing a bit quieter than before. “I made a shitload of money and I never managed to find anything significant to spend it on, so I mostly used my funds to be a general nuisance”

Henry finally lights his cigar and draws on it, letting the smoke fill his lungs for a few seconds before letting it out through his nose. He closes his eyes, enjoying the familiarity of it.

“I suppose all that money isn’t going to help me here, and I severely doubt blondie over there accepts cheques” He says with a small chuckle, jabbing his thumb over his shoulder towards Maximilian vont Blitz.

“It doesn’t matter though, I have… other skills” Henry smiles genuinely, clearly reliving some fond memory. “But enough about me, what about you? You seem to be part of the upper crust as well. Do you find it as mind numbingly boring as I do?”

Archibald Don Castro

“Selling vacuums? I see. Those sure must’ve been some expensive appliances if you could earn a fortune from that.” He smirks, but still looks genuinely impressed. “As a fellow man of wealth, it came to me primarily by inheritance. My grandfather Bertram Don Castro pioneered the steam travel industry with easy to obtain locomotives. The profits were passed down to my father and then me once he passed away.”

The Count ponders Henry’s question while scratching his sideburns. “Boring? Hmmm, yes and no. I don’t regret my fortune. I do however resent other aristocrats. They tend to be some of the most pretentious, corrupt, cowardly ne’er do wells I’ve come to know!”

“You know, I respect you Henry.” He folds his arms with an approving nod. “You say it how it is. Regardless of how petty your motives might be, at least you actually do something with your spare time. I never have respect for other fat cats who lay on their nest egg just to hold a position in power. Or worse, they aid in a useless bureaucracy. Someday…” He halts and shakes his head. Once composed, his expression now looks bitter and disgusted.

Henry Hoover

Henry’s eyes light up with surprise, and his smile grows wider, into something more genuine than before. It looks unnatural on his face, it’s obvious Henry does not smile often.

“And here I was worried we wouldn’t get along. I hate snooty pricks in their glass towers! I’d pay good money to see them torn down.” Henry’s grip on his golf club tightens.

“I have, on occasion.” he adds, with a predatory glint in his eye.

Henry turns his attention to his solid gold wristwatch, and he takes it off, dangling it in front of Archibald’s face. “I only bought this stupid watch because it’s the only one of its kind. Something about the clockmaker dying as he made it. It’s the sort of shit my ‘friends’ would have a seizure over.”

Henry holds up the watch up to his own face, a faint yellow reflection visible as the watch catches the light.

“It’s awful. It’s ugly and heavy and doesn’t even tell the time properly. So I bought it. I find it quite the adequate description of the ‘aristocrat’ life; expensive, useless and an eyesore to anyone in their right mind.”

Henry puts the watch back on. “It also pissed off that asshole Greg Barbour more than you can possibly imagine. Especially once he learned I don’t even take it off when I shower.”

Archibald Don Castro

Archibald looks at the watch intently. There doesn’t seem to be any enthusiasm nor disinterest in his reaction. “That’s certainly a watch. I’ve never been the sort to buy fancy goods for the mere sake of it. I prefer more… philanthropic investments. Even so, the fact you succeeded in getting a rise out of your foes is a riot! I can only imagine the priceless look on their faces!” The gentleman snickers at the thought.

Henry Hoover

Henry’s smile falters slightly.

“Once you have enough money, ‘for the sake of it’ is the only reason you have to spend it.”

Henry pauses, as if unsure of something.

“450 billion pounds.” He emphasises the ‘b’ in billion. “You can’t even wrap your head around such a stupid number. That’s more than the number of stars in the galaxy. At least the one where I’m from.”

Henry’s gaze hardens, and he looks warily back at the count after snapping out of his tangent.

“A philanthropist. I’ve met more than my share of philanthropists in my life. What do you spend your wealth on?”

Hail to the King

arrow_drop_down# Poor Unfortunate Granny

Harrow

Of all the people forced to participate in the prisoner death game, the sight of the old woman made Harrow’s blood boil. The way her eyes squinted, her voice mumbling something about sleep and tea, made the ex-centurion feel pity for this unfortunate granny. Could she even…see? See well enough to protect herself from the events to come, or even worse, enough that she could transcribe exactly what the letters told them all? Did she have any idea what was going on or what was most likely about to happen to her? That these coming days were to be a literal fight for one's planet, not just saving your own soul, but the life and safety of everyone you love back home? How…how could someone from any corner of the universe find pleasure and joy in making someone like her fight for their own life? Harrow had heard tales of ancient god’s on her own world, some of which were considered evil, but she never really believed they existed. But now…she wasn’t so sure.

The woman cautiously steps toward the frail figure, trying to make herself appear as gentle as possible, but finding it hard to hide the scowl on her lips.

“Excuse me, ma’am? Are you…are you alright?! Do you know why you are here?” She spoke in a slightly louder octave than normal to be sure the woman could hear her correctly, placing a kind blackened left hand on the woman's forearm.
