Harrow

A dull, but distant guise paints her face. It appears…calm, numb to the party, eyes seeming to look past everything and everyone, gazing at something beyond the atmosphere of the room. Yet, while her expression gives off a semi-relaxed visage, Harrow’s body appears otherwise. Her fists are clenched, the muscles in her arms tensed, her posture contrasting with the guise of her face. Putting two and two together -the envelope containing tonight's instructions crinkled between tense right handed fingers- it is clear that she is not just looking past the room, but lost in some memory freezing her in place.

She wears a simple dress, if you'd call a strappy gold ensemble simple (https://i.imgur.com/htq9T6d.png). Silk wisps wrap around her chest and up her back where they meet at her shoulders and descend, shimmering strands caught by a gentle breeze. A rose bushel of hair finds itself tied together by its own strands in a bun atop her head, exposing the defined musculature to her back. Double pink locks frame her face and trail down the front of her figure. Elegant, yet uncomplicated, and easy to move in.

Eventually, with an obviously shaking inhale of air, Harrow moves to a vacant chair at an abandoned table and falls onto its frame. She looks down at the letter held in her right hand, while her left clutches at her moistened forehead. For a moment, her attention turns to where Maxamillion is in the room, a desperate gaze to her eyes. She looks down at the letter once more, then to Max, then the letter, stuck in a loop of endlessly rereading its contents.

She was 15. She begged me not to do it but I...I was a bounty hunter with a master to please. She was a runaway, a 'criminal' escaped from a testing facility and it was my prerogative to bring her back, or kill her if she wouldn't comply."

She looks at the envelope containing the secret now free in the open air, her fingers smoothing out the creases nervously. "She didn't comply. So I did what I was instructed to do," her voice croaks.

Harrow looks at Seseri, a pleading glint in her eyes, "Perhaps killing someone as a mercy isn't such a bad thing? Considering, at the time, your intentions were honorable?" She smiles at Seseri sincerely.

Seseri

"I'm sorry that you had to go through that... poor girl." Seseri closes her eyes and sighs softly. "I definitely thought it was a mercy at the time. She was... a young girl by the name of Eira, a teenager really. She had the heart of an explorer, like us, but she had more heart than sense. She went exploring the shroud without proper training and by the time any proper rescue reached her, it was too late. She had been twisted and mutated by the corruptive darkness which blankets our world... her inner flame extinguished, parasitic growths covering her. As far as we know... there is no way to cure that kind of corruption, and every moment would've been agony for her. So I put her out of her misery... my note says she could've been saved. That I cut her life short for nothing." Seseri shudders as she hands Harrow the note.

Harrow

She didn't expect such openness, Seseri actually handing Harrow the note to see for herself. So, Harrow did the same, trading her crinkled letter for Seseri's. On Harrow's note, at the bottom, you notice the words, You took her name, and never mourned her. Her family never knew what happened.

"Seseri...it seems you and I share similar secrets. Young girls, teenagers, lives cut too short." A sigh ripples through Harrow's chest, her shoulders shaking with grief. "As sad as I am to know that we share a similar guilt, I’m strangely comforted by this. You know, I also wish, knowing what I struggled through, that such things were never forced on us - that we never had to live in a timeline where endring these weight's were our's to bear." Harrow pat's Seseri's hand.

"The note says she could have been saved, yes, but...at the time, you didn't know that, did you? Taking a life should never be easy, but if you had never heard of a cure before, even if one existed, you can't hold that against yourself. Can I ask though, if you have any idea how could she have been saved? Or is that part of the mystery that this letter plagues you with?"

arrow_drop_down# Exchanging Pleasantries

Ami Muscaria

Ami saunters over to the table Harrow is occupying and takes a seat across from her. "You look lovely," she clears her throat before continuing. "I don't believe we got the chance to meet before, but my name's Ami. How are you holding up?"

Harrow

A mournful chuckle escapes her lips. She doesn't look up immediantely. "Not very well Ami...the contense of the letter...the secret we have to tell others, its something I've never told anyone - much less a stranger. Time is waisting and I am finding it harder and harder to reveal..." She crinkles the note she was just reading in between a clenched fist and heaves a heavy sigh.

Finally, she looks up at you, down, and then back up, a weary smile painting her face. "You look lovely too Ami...are you enjoying the party? Danced with anyone interesting? I'm Harrow by the way," the woman extends a scorched left hand to you in greeting.

Ami Muscaria

Ami takes Harrow's hand, careful to be gentle. "I know how you feel. I'm... not exactly sure how I feel about telling someone a secret I've kept close for so long, especially in this type of circumstance."

Harrow

The woman meets Ami's grasp, equally as gentle, yet there is a touch starved desperation in her clutch. "Well...if It would help you...I could go first. Believe me, after you hear mine, I doubt you will feel so ashamed of your own," her lips curl into a sympathetic smile.

Seseri

Seseri slowly walks into the room, clutching the side of her head, her free hand holding her now-removed mask. Under her mask her eyes can be seen glowing a deep red, her face squinting in slight pain.

Finding a comfortable-looking chair, Seseri unceremoniously collapses on top of it and looks around the room.

arrow_drop_down# Are you alright?

Xerio

Xerio walks over to Seseri after she collapses into her chair," Long first event?" He has brought over a cup of water and offers it to her.

Seseri

Seseri chuckles softly as she chugs down the water, before scribbling down on her pad. "I'll say."

Maximillian von Blitz

The music stops.

Maximillian suddenly rises from his throne. Silently, he begins to descend from his perch high above the dancefloor. With every dozen steps a new person followed behind the ruler, culminating into another conga line of the boys. Shortly after, new music begins to play throughout the hall.

The room flashes with a brilliant light that casts shadows across the entire party hall. Outside the ship, whichever world they had been orbiting for the past day had been struck by something truly disastrous and was now thrust into the rapid process of its own obliteration. The explosive spectacle sent chunks of rock and magma every which way. Some collide into the ship only to be vaporized on contact by some sort of force field. Every person onboard was getting front row tickets to this hapless world's annihilation.

Almost as suddenly as all of this began, the world was all but gone, minus a lingering debris field quickly scattering into space. In an instant the ship orbited a new world, and again, it, like the last world, was destroyed in much the same fashion. With each world's destruction came a flash of its unique identifier along the ship's window panes. In that vein, every contender in Maximillian's abhorrent game knew at that point the identification of their own world -- "Earth-" followed by a string of numbers and letters.

Fortunately, no world belonging to the current players met such a terrible fate... yet. After nearly twenty minutes of awful destruction the ship began to cycle through each of the champion's worlds one after another, viewing it from orbit for one minute before cycling to the next, repeating until the night finally arrived.

Grug

Grug climbs some stairs, up to a balcony, overlooking the massive window, watching the destruction of worlds. He wears nothing but swim trunks, still dripping wet from his excursion with Yumi.

"Please, grant me the music of the gods for this!" He shouts to no one in particular, as he turns back around to face the rest of the passengers, his arms lifted high in the air. He freezes in that moment for several seconds, but is blessed as someone, who knows who, begins to play music.

"Grug is here to let all of you know! Grug is mighty! Grug will not allow Maximilian to destroy his world! For the Gods he will prove his world is perfect! As he stands here, this will not be the last you all see of Grug! He will be there, greeting the survivors at the end! He will not go quietly, and he will save his world!"

Grug pauses momentarily. "Grug wishes for the survival of as many as possible, but knows not everyone will be able to make it. For everyone who can survive, Grug will be happy to meet your friends and family who you will save from the wrath of Maximilian before he is moved to the next round to fight once again and prove the perfection of his home! May they all meet Grug, Grug the genius! Grug the eventual victor, no matter how many games he is forced to play, Grug will rise above as he always has, like no other man! To die this night is not even a consideration for Grug, for none here are mightier than he!" He clenches a fist, raising that arm higher, lowering his other arm.

"To Grug's victory! In the words of these Gods, 'Prosit!'" Grug mimes throwing a glass down with his clenched hand.

Suddenly, his shoulders slump. "And to all who must fight for their lives and their homes and their Earths tonight... good luck."

Grug leaves the balcony much less bombastic than he was before, speed-walking down the stairs.

arrow_drop_down# Prosit!

Ami Muscaria

Ami, still shaken by witnessing the destruction of worlds outside the ship, with a few tears running down her face, lifts up one hand in consolidation and shouts, "Prosit! To all who can beat the odds!"

arrow_drop_down# a hero's sendoff

Mabel Sinclair

Mabel watches Grug off with her hands clasped at her chest. She's still in shock over the cacophony of worlds being destroyed, but resolutely hung onto his every word.

"Prosit, Grug... I wish the best for you, your people, and... your loved ones."

Hail to the King
